<span style="font-size:16px;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Teclast F15 Notebook 15.6 inch</span></strong><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Teclast F15 Notebook 15.6 inch</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">&nbsp;is a perfect Notebook for your daily use. Equipped with a&nbsp;</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">15.6 inch 1920 x 1080 IPS screen,</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">&nbsp;brings your photos and videos to life.&nbsp;</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Windows 10 OS</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">ensures you more wonderful user experience. Powered by&nbsp;</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Intel N4100 Quad Core processor,</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">&nbsp;offers you smooth operation and stable multitasking experience.&nbsp;</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">1.0MP camera</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">&nbsp;for capturing memorable moments and high quality pictures in daily life. Featuring&nbsp;</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Intel UHD Graphics 600 GPU,</span><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">&nbsp;all of this give gamers a full suite for gaming dominance and offer gamers a truly seamless gaming experience.&nbsp;</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Main Features:</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">1. Windows 10 OS</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Offers more powerful performance, brings you more smooth and wonderful user experience</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">2. Intel N4100 Quad Core 1.1GHz, up to 2.4GHz</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Ultra-low-voltage platform and Quad Core processing provide maximum high-efficiency power</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">3. Intel UHD Graphics 600 GPU</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">On-processor graphics with shared video memory provide high image quality for Internet use, basic photo editing and casual gaming</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">4. 15.6 inch 1920 x 1080 IPS Screen</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Offers good experience for watching videos and browsing the Web&nbsp;</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">5. 8GB RAM DDR4 for Advanced Multitasking</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Substantial high-bandwidth RAM to smoothly run your games, photos and video-editing applications</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">6. 256GB SSD Storage Capacity</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Provides room to store pictures, videos, music and more</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">7. 1.0MP Camera for Photos and Face-to-Face Chat</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">Allow you to capture memorable moments or chat with friends</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">8. Micro HDMI Output</span><br style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">
<span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102); font-family: arial;">You can connect the device to high-definition monitor or projector</span></span><div id="specification_end"></div>

    <p>This warranty and return policy are only available for the sub-categories of&nbsp;laptops, netbooks, and mini PC.</p><p><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong>1 year warranty&nbsp;&nbsp;</strong></span></p><p>If the product is defective within one year from its delivery date, customers can return it for a free repair.</p><p>The scope of this warranty excludes all damages caused by artificial factors, like dis-assembly, misuse, drops, falls, water, unofficial firmwares, software modifications or similar causes both for computers&nbsp;and their accessories.</p><p>If your return request has been approved, we will cover the entire repair fee, handling fee and the replacement of the defective component.</p><p>If one or more of its accessories are faulty within 3 months from their delivery date, we can arrange a replacement or a refund after confirming the nature of the problem. In order to do so, please send us some photos or a video of the issue.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong>Return policy</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><strong>DOA (Defective on arrival)</strong></span></p><p>If the product arrives broken, please contact us within&nbsp;7 days after receiving it and follow the instructions shown in the&nbsp;7 Days Product Guarantee.</p><p>Due to the fact that computers are to be considered high-value items, we may ask you to return the defective product before receiving a replacement or a refund.</p><p><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt;">14&nbsp;Days Dislike Products</span></strong></p><p>If you are not satisfied with the computer you received, please contact us within&nbsp;14 days from its delivery date and send us some photos or a short video showing the product and why you dislike it.<br><br>You can return it after receiving our confirmation, and will have to pay the return shipping fees.<br><br>We will refund the price you paid after receiving the computer. We will also ensure that all its original accessories have been returned and that the computer has no damages or scratches. If there are any aesthetic imperfections or missing parts, we will charge you 20% of the computer's price.<br><br><strong>Note:</strong> you will be responsible for paying all the customs charges and import duties occurred when returning the product. We will deduct the taxes we had to pay from the refund amount.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt;">Broken Within One Month</span></strong></p><p>If the computer appears to be defective within one month from its delivery date and the cause is related to its manufacturing process, we can arrange a refund, replacement, free repair or local maintenance based on its problem.<br><br>If the problem is caused by the computer itself, we can arrange a refund or a replacement according to your preferences after sending it back to us. We will cover the postage that you send the product back only if it is less than $60 USD.</p><p><br>We can offer you other forms of compensation in case the problem can be solved in other ways, as by upgrading the software or the version of the system.<br><br>The scope of this warranty excludes all damages caused by artificial factors, like dis-assembly, misuse, drops, falls, water, unofficial firmwares, software modifications or similar causes both for computers and their accessories.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong>Broken After One Month And Within One Year</strong></span></p><p>If the computer appears to be faulty after one month but within one year after its delivery date and the problem is caused by its manufacturing process, you are eligible for receiving a free repair of this product.<br>Please send us some photos or a video of the issue. If your return request has been approved, we will send you the return shipping address and other instructions.<br>After receiving the defective product and after it has been repaired, we will send it back to you with a free shipping method. We will then issue a 50% refund of the return shipping fees if they cost more than $15 but less than $60. We will not cover these fees if their cost exceeds these values.<br>The scope of this warranty excludes all damages caused by artificial factors, like dis-assembly, misuse, drops, falls, water, unofficial firmwares, software modifications or similar causes both for computers and their accessories.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong>Local maintenance</strong></span></p><p>If you do not want to pay the high return shipping fees, you can find a repair shop in your country.<br>Please enquire about the estimated repair fees and inform us about this value before actually starting to repair the product.<br>We can pay the repair fees only if their cost does not exceed 30% of the computer’s price and is below $40 in total. We will otherwise request you to return the product and allow us to fix it for free in our repair centers.<br>If the repairers can not guarantee that the computer can be fixed or need to disassemble it for assessing the nature of the problem, please ensure that they will not damage the product during the whole process.<br>If you send the product back to us for a free repair, we will ask you to pay an extra repair fee after inspecting and determining that there have been further damages caused by a third party.<br>If you are sure to be able to fix this problem, we can send you a replacement of one or more components or accessories. However, you should not damage this item during the whole process. We will ask you to pay an extra repair fee after inspecting and determining that the product has been further damaged. Unless you are confident and have the skills to repair it, we do not recommend trying to fix it yourself.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Notes:</strong></p><p>- Please&nbsp;contact us&nbsp;before returning a defective item; otherwise the return process may be delayed.<br>- We can arrange a refund or a replacement of the product after receiving the defective item and confirming that it is indeed defective;<br>- The return shipping fees will be at the customer’s expense, except in case of DOA cases;The return shipping fee of the defective product must be discussed and agreed upon before you send the product back. Or we will not be responsible for any return shipping costs.</p><p>- The return shipping fee of the defective product must be discussed and agreed upon before you send the product back. Or we will not be responsible for any return shipping costs.</p><p>- We are not responsible for paying any customs fees for return shipping or for shipping back to you</p><p>- If you do not want to pay high import duties on the return package, please avoid selecting an express mail service like DHL, UPS, TNT, FedEx, and similar ones;</p><p><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: #333333;">- If you refuse delivery of a parcel due to import duties or taxes, you assume all liability for all costs involved in returning the item to us.</span><br><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: #333333;">- You are also liable for any import duties or taxes incurred during the return process.Click&nbsp;<a style="color: #333333;" href="../Insurances_hl69_at650">here</a>&nbsp;to view more.</span></p><p><br>- Please include a note inside the return package by including the following details (this will accelerate your return request):<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; your order number;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; the product ID or name and the quantity;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; a short description of the problem occurred with this product;<br>- If you encounter any difficulties in returning a product, please do not hesitate to contact us to discuss other forms of compensation;<br>- If the defect on the product is not related to its manufacturing process, the customer should pay the return shipping fees.</p>
